   function show(message1)
       {
          new1=window.open("","教室資訊","location,status,resizable=yes,width=600,height=100");
          new1.document.write (message1);
       }
   function show_close()
       {
           new1.close();
       }
 </script>

<script language="JavaScript" type="text/JavaScript">

function ChangeSelectA(form)
{
    var objSelect=form.dpt_sel;
    selvar=objSelect.options[objSelect.selectedIndex].value;
    for(i=0;i&lt;form.dptname.length;i++)
    {
        if(form.dptname.options[i].value == selvar)
        {
            form.dptname.selectedIndex=i;
            break;
        }
    }
}
function ChangeSelectB(form)
{
    var objSelect=form.dptname;
    selvar=objSelect.options[objSelect.selectedIndex].value;
    for(i=0;i&lt;form.dpt_sel.length;i++)
    {
        if(form.dpt_sel.options[i].value.charAt(0) == selvar.charAt(0))
        {
            form.dpt_sel.selectedIndex=i;
            break;
        }
    }
    sem_onchange();
}
function changeyear(form)
{
    var objSelect=form.yearcode;
    var objdpt=form.dptname;
    selvar=objdpt.options[objdpt.selectedIndex].value;
    sem_onchange();
}
function daycheck() {
    var obj_time = document.getElementsByName("alltime");
    var check1 = document.getElementById("week1");
    var check2 = document.getElementById("week2");
    var check3 = document.getElementById("week3");
    var check4 = document.getElementById("week4");
    var check5 = document.getElementById("week5");
    var check6 = document.getElementById("week6");
    if(check1.checked||check2.checked||check3.checked||check4.checked||check5.checked||check6.checked){
        obj_time[0].checked = false;
        obj_time[1].checked = true;
    }
}
//加選方式
function selcheck() {
    var obj_sel = document.getElementsByName("allsel");
    var check1 = document.getElementById("selCode1");
    var check2 = document.getElementById("selCode2");
    var check3 = document.getElementById("selCode3");
  
    if(check1.checked||check2.checked||check3.checked){
        obj_sel[0].checked = false;
        obj_sel[1].checked = true;
    }
}
function procedcheck() {
    var obj_proced = document.getElementsByName("allproced");
    var check0 = document.getElementById("proced0");
    var check1 = document.getElementById("proced1");
    var check2 = document.getElementById("proced2");
    var check3 = document.getElementById("proced3");
    var check4 = document.getElementById("proced4");
    var checkE = document.getElementById("procedE");
    var check5 = document.getElementById("proced5");
    var check6 = document.getElementById("proced6");
    var check7 = document.getElementById("proced7");
    var check8 = document.getElementById("proced8");
    var check9 = document.getElementById("proced9");
    var checkA = document.getElementById("procedA");
    var checkB = document.getElementById("procedB");
    var checkC = document.getElementById("procedC");
    var checkD = document.getElementById("procedD");

    if(check0.checked||check1.checked||check2.checked||check3.checked||check4.checked||checkE.checked ||check5.checked||check6.checked||check7.checked||check8.checked||check9.checked||checkA.checked ||checkB.checked||checkC.checked||checkD.checked){
        obj_proced[0].checked = false;
        obj_proced[1].checked = true;
    }
}

function timeradio() {
    var obj_time = document.getElementsByName("alltime");
    var check1 = document.getElementById("week1");
    var check2 = document.getElementById("week2");
    var check3 = document.getElementById("week3");
    var check4 = document.getElementById("week4");
    var check5 = document.getElementById("week5");
    var check6 = document.getElementById("week6");
    if(obj_time[0].checked){//不限時間
        check1.checked = check2.checked = check3.checked = check4.checked = check5.checked = check6.checked = false;
    }
}
//加選方式
function selectradio() {
    var obj_sel = document.getElementsByName("allsel");
    var check1 = document.getElementById("selCode1");
    var check2 = document.getElementById("selCode2");
    var check3 = document.getElementById("selCode3");
  
    if(obj_sel[0].checked){//不限
        check1.checked = check2.checked = check3.checked  = false;
    }
}
function procedradio() {
    var obj_proced = document.getElementsByName("allproced");
    var check0 = document.getElementById("proced0");
    var check1 = document.getElementById("proced1");
    var check2 = document.getElementById("proced2");
    var check3 = document.getElementById("proced3");
    var check4 = document.getElementById("proced4");
    var checkE = document.getElementById("procedE");
    var check5 = document.getElementById("proced5");
    var check6 = document.getElementById("proced6");
    var check7 = document.getElementById("proced7");
    var check8 = document.getElementById("proced8");
    var check9 = document.getElementById("proced9");
    var checkA = document.getElementById("procedA");
    var checkB = document.getElementById("procedB");
    var checkC = document.getElementById("procedC");
    var checkD = document.getElementById("procedD");

    if(obj_proced[0].checked){//不限時間
        check0.checked = check1.checked = check2.checked = check3.checked = check4.checked = checkE.checked =check5.checked = check6.checked = check7.checked = check8.checked = check9.checked = checkA.checked = checkB.checked = checkC.checked = checkD.checked =  false;
    }
}
function sem_onchange() {
    var objsel = document.getElementById("select_sem");
    var obj_dpt = document.getElementById("dptname");
    var obj_top = document.getElementById("dpt_sel");   
	var obj_page=document.getElementById("page_cnt");
    var obj_coursename = document.getElementById("coursename");
    var obj_teacher = document.getElementById("teachername");
    var obj_year = document.getElementById("yearcode");
    var obj_selcode = document.getElementsByName("selcode");
    var selcode;
    for (var i=0; i&lt; obj_selcode.length;i++){
        if (obj_selcode[i].checked) {
            selcode = obj_selcode[i].value;
            break;
        }
    }   
    var obj_time = document.getElementsByName("alltime");
    var alltime;
    for (var i=0; i&lt; obj_time.length;i++){
        if (obj_time[i].checked) {
            alltime = obj_time[i].value;
            break;
        }
    }           
    var week1=week2=week3=week4=week5=week6="";
    if(document.getElementById("week1").checked)
        week1 = document.getElementById("week1").value;
    if(document.getElementById("week2").checked)
        week2 = document.getElementById("week2").value;
    if(document.getElementById("week3").checked)
        week3 = document.getElementById("week3").value;
    if(document.getElementById("week4").checked)
        week4 = document.getElementById("week4").value;
    if(document.getElementById("week5").checked)
        week5 = document.getElementById("week5").value;
    if(document.getElementById("week6").checked)
        week6 = document.getElementById("week6").value;

     var obj_proced = document.getElementsByName("allproced");
    var allproced;
    for (var i=0; i&lt; obj_proced.length;i++){
        if (obj_proced[i].checked) {
            allproced = obj_proced[i].value;
            break;
        }
    }           
    var proced0=proced1=proced2=proced3=proced4=procedE=proced5=proced6=proced7=proced8=proced9=procedA=procedB=procedC=procedD="";
     if(document.getElementById("proced0").checked)
        proced0 = document.getElementById("proced0").value;
     if(document.getElementById("proced1").checked)
        proced1 = document.getElementById("proced1").value;
     if(document.getElementById("proced2").checked)
        proced2 = document.getElementById("proced2").value;
     if(document.getElementById("proced3").checked)
        proced3 = document.getElementById("proced3").value;
     if(document.getElementById("proced4").checked)
        proced4 = document.getElementById("proced4").value;
     if(document.getElementById("procedE").checked)
        procedE = document.getElementById("procedE").value;
     if(document.getElementById("proced5").checked)
        proced5 = document.getElementById("proced5").value;
     if(document.getElementById("proced6").checked)
        proced6 = document.getElementById("proced6").value;
     if(document.getElementById("proced7").checked)
        proced7 = document.getElementById("proced7").value;
     if(document.getElementById("proced8").checked)
        proced8 = document.getElementById("proced8").value;
     if(document.getElementById("proced9").checked)
        proced9 = document.getElementById("proced9").value;
     if(document.getElementById("procedA").checked)
        procedA = document.getElementById("procedA").value;
     if(document.getElementById("procedB").checked)
        procedB = document.getElementById("procedB").value;
     if(document.getElementById("procedC").checked)
        procedC = document.getElementById("procedC").value;
     if(document.getElementById("procedD").checked)
        procedD = document.getElementById("procedD").value;
    
	var obj_sel = document.getElementsByName("allsel");
    var allsel;
    for (var i=0; i&lt; obj_sel.length;i++){
        if (obj_sel[i].checked) {
            allsel = obj_sel[i].value;
            break;
        }
    }           
    var selCode1=selCode2=selCode3="";
    if(document.getElementById("selCode1").checked)
        selCode1 = document.getElementById("selCode1").value;
    if(document.getElementById("selCode2").checked)
        selCode2 = document.getElementById("selCode2").value;
    if(document.getElementById("selCode3").checked)
        selCode3 = document.getElementById("selCode3").value;

    var url="search_for_02_dpt.php?current_sem="+objsel.options[objsel.selectedIndex].value+"&amp;coursename="+obj_coursename.value+"&amp;dptname="+obj_dpt.options[obj_dpt.selectedIndex].value+"&amp;dpt_sel="+obj_top.options[obj_top.selectedIndex].value+"&amp;yearcode="+obj_year.options[obj_year.selectedIndex].value+"&amp;teachername="+obj_teacher.value+"&amp;selcode="+selcode+"&amp;alltime="+alltime+"&amp;week1="+week1+"&amp;week2="+week2+"&amp;week3="+week3+"&amp;week4="+week4+"&amp;week5="+week5+"&amp;week6="+week6+"&amp;allproced="+allproced+"&amp;proced0="+proced0+"&amp;proced1="+proced1+"&amp;proced2="+proced2+"&amp;proced3="+proced3+"&amp;proced4="+proced4+"&amp;procedE="+procedE+"&amp;proced5="+proced5+"&amp;proced6="+proced6+"&amp;proced7="+proced7+"&amp;proced8="+proced8+"&amp;proced9="+proced9+"&amp;procedA="+procedA+"&amp;procedB="+procedB+"&amp;procedC="+procedC+"&amp;procedD="+procedD+"&amp;allsel="+allsel+"&amp;selCode1="+selCode1+"&amp;selCode2="+selCode2+"&amp;selCode3="+selCode3+"&amp;page_cnt="+obj_page.value;
    window.location = url;
}
//--&gt;
</script>

<script language="JavaScript">

var window_schedule = '';

function schedule_add(cid)
{
    if (!window_schedule.closed &amp;&amp; window_schedule.location)
        window_schedule.location.href = 'myschedule.php?add='+cid;
    else
        window_schedule=window.open('myschedule.php?add='+cid,'schedule','height=500,width=730,scrollbars=yes,resizable=yes');
        
    if (window.focus) {window_schedule.focus()}
    return false;
}

</script>
